In the absence of user ratings, the system assigns a composite score based on the disease importance and the news volume associated with the alert. If a location's marker has multiple alerts, the color associated with the most prominent alert is used.<\/p><h5>Marker Size<\/h5><p>The large circle indicates a country-level alert, while state, province and local alerts are indicated by the small circle.<\/p><\/section><\/div>","zoom_lat":15,"zoom_lon":18,"zoom_level":3}
